AMAZWI OMLOBI 
  Angizukuthetha bulanda ngoba angiganisi. Noma-ke bengiganisa bengingebuthethe kepha bengiyothi, "Nina basekuthini tholani ithambo lami." Ngiqhubeke ngithi, "Uma umntanamr enihlupha nize ningibikele. Mina ukumazi kwami kuphelele ekutheni akaguli ndawo." 
  Umlando wempilo yezulu nomhlaba uyaguquguquka uphendulwa yizimeko ngezikhathi lezo; kuhle kweselwa liphendulwa yinhlabathi. Ngivunyelwe yisikhathi ukuba ngibambe iqhaza kllbakhi abasilobele izincwadi eziyisabelo nefa lezizukulwane ezisayoqhuma, zitshaleke, zikhule, zithelc kwaMhlaba. Isivivane asibekelwe mncele ukuthi abaphonsi baphosa umgubane kuphela, kepha sibuthela umkhumenge, insengetshe, ichoba, itshe-nso, igwadle nokunye okwaziyo nawe. Kunjalo-ke nasesivivaneni sezincwadi zabalobi bezizwe zingaka nje entendeni yobuso bomhlaba. 
  Kuzinjongo kubalobi bengakaya ukuhlandlela kwabo emsebenzini osunezinkulungwane zeminyaka kwaqala ukulotshwa izincwadi. Kepha lIkuqonda nokwazi kwami kuyafinyelela ekutheni umqukuthu womlobi yiwo lowo wokudlulisela kubafundi' lokho akucaban'gile. Sekumfikele wakuloba; nanjengomuntu othuka inhlamba emkhandlwini. Ngithi-ke kinina bafundi nantoke usikothi olwalwenziwa, lukhulunywa ngobabamkhulu. 
  Umhlaba nabantu bawo uyaguga uphele, kepha ukubonga akugugi, akupheli, kuhlala kuyiklumela njalo nje nangale kwezimbiza zezulu. Ngibonga ikhehla uMnu. Ngcobo waseClermont Township okunguyena owangishiyela ngabhema ngencla ngeNkosi uMpande nabaNtwana bakhe. Abanye abanginongisa ngesinongo semiqondo nolwazi Iwabo oluphusile yilaba; uMnu. A. 1, Mdlalose waseLokishini labantu eDumbe. Sengathithi isipho sakhe sokwelekelela abantu singakhula nasemsebenzini wakhe wobufundisi. Ngibonga. uDan Dhladhla, noSydney Thokozani lali, nomama uNkosikazi kaMhloli wezikole uMnu. S. M. Nhlapho onolwazi olungale kwezitsha ezincwadini zoMdlalo (Drama). Ngingasho ukuthi wangibhibhidlisa ngisabhibhidla nalencwadi ngaze ngaqhuma amabamba. Ngibonga futhi nakuMnu. W. O. 

 

DlIbazane. Ungomllnye wababethi angigiye njalo noma kllngasekho ongishoyo noma kllngasekho abananela isisho sami. Ngingemlibale uMnu. Thomas VlIsi Dlamini osebenza kwaKhomlshani eClermont Township. Nguye owayengihambela njalo ekuguleni kwami okllnxa-mbili. Phela lencwadi iyincwadi yokuqala engayibhala ekllbuyeni kwami esibhedlela eKhingi. Ngangiyisigulana sasekhaya esasesilashwa nguNdombo, intombazane yesibili eza emva kwami. Ekungivakasheleni kwakhe uMnu T. V. Dlamini kwaku ukubuza impilo, 'okwesibili sixoxe kabanzi ngokuhlcla lencwadi esiyisihlangu esesiyozivikela ngaso uma kukhulunywa usikothi Iwesizwe sabaNsundu. 
  Ngibonga futhi uMnu. N. P. Kunenc onguMhloli wezikole esifundcni sakwaHlathikhulu, kwaNgwane. Ngingesibale isisa ncsasasa engalithola ohambcni, ekuhlanganeni nasekukhulumeni kwethu noMnu. N. P. Kunene. Nguye-ke owangihlelela kahlc izindawo ezaziphundulckile ngesiSwazi, ehlandlela kulezo cngangizilotshelwc nguMaMotha, iNdlunkulu yami. 
  Abokugcina okudinga ngibabonge yiNdlunkulu yami eyabe ilokhu inginakashele ithi kanti Iczizincwadi ezokwcnzani uma sengizifundela mina ngcdwa inguyazane. Wanginakashcla lwaze lwaphela uvalo oluhlupha abalobi ukuthi izwe lizothi, "Ubcndc lolul" Uma akuyanga ngaye ngabe zahlala imindundu kwaze kwalala nobulwembu kuzo. Akuscnzekanga-ke. Ngabe sengiyithumel a kuMhleli uMnu. C. L. S. Nyembezi kwaShuter & Shooter okllnguyena oyiphumclelisilc ckugxotshwcni. Wakhombisa nomdlandla wakhe ongenamkhawulo ngokuba izingxoxo ezikuyo zandulelwc yisethulo esilotshwc nguyc. 
Bethucl Blose Ndclu (UNonkamfela) 
ISETHULO 
  Isicclo sikaMnu. Ndclu ukuba nami ngiphosc libe linyc 10k wethula lomzamo wakhc ngisamukele ngenhliziyo emhlophe. Siyakwazi sonke ukuthi ziseyingcosana kakhulu izincwadi cziyimidlalo ezilotshwc ngolimi IwcsiZulu. Azifiki naseshumini. Kungakho-kc ngithe lapho ngiyibona lencwadi ngaba nokuthokoza.okukhulu. Kodwa akusikho lokho kuphela. Ngilithandile ikhono likaNdclu ekusidwebclcni lomfanekiso wakhe. Usithatha amuke nathi, sizibone scsikhona cnkundlcni ycNkonjan' edukel' czulwini. Nathi kube sengathi sesiyayibona iNdlov' enesihlonti ilabalabela ubukhosi bukaZulu kanti izobhema ikholwe lapho esegadla uMagwaz' . eguqile njengetholc. 
  Scsikwcjwayele ukuba sithi lapho sibona izincwadi czilotshwe ngcsiZulu sithi wo, yizincwadi zezinganc zcsikole. Akukho lutho olungabathokozisa abadala. Lena-kc Zulu akusiyo njc incwadi yabantwana besikole. Yincwadi kaZulu jikelcle omdala nomncane. Nabadala angingabazi mina ukuthi kuyobathokozisa ukukubukela ukugiya kwalensizwa cngethemba ukuthi isazobuye ihlabane Zulu.

Mpande: Leliwisa engaligawulelwa yisizwe Liyangisinda, anginamandla okuliphatha. Ngikhumbula lifika nezikhulu nezinduna, Lafika liluhlaza lagcotshwa unwali,

Makha: Zikuhalalisele izinduna nezikhulu nxashana zikhumbula uhambo Iwazo zinqamula izinkangala, iziphondo ziyaphansi emahlanzeni, zifike zigawule umnweba eziwukhombiswe uNonkomba kaNomkhubulwane, zibuye nawo umanzi ziwuklaye zikhiphe umongo, ukuze kuthi ekuvuthweni kwalo lingaklayeki kodwa lihlale liyilo elithandwa iZinyane leSilo. 
Mpande: Makhasana, awuzwa engikuhlosile. 
Wena ukhuluma ngewisa olibonayo Leli eliphanyekwe lapha emgibeni. Mina ngikhuluma ngaloCetshwayo Osephethwe yindelelo enkulu lapha; Ngisho lapha emzini wami Makhasana. Mina-ke ngithi, angisalithandi leliwisa. 
Makha: Ndabezitha ngiyezwa; ngiyezwa ngokungalithandi kwakho leliwisa othi liwisa umuzi wakho Ndaba, ngendelelo yokuthi phela nakhu selithophele, akusensuku zatshwala. 
Mpande: Ngife, athathe uhukhosi bakwaZulu! 
Qha; ngeke ukubone lokho Makhasana. INkosi kithi kayibekwa ngamkhaba. Kumele uCetshwayo abuthathe ngezikhali Ngoba mina ngibona - iNdlov' enesihlonti.
